        <img src="/img/auth-login.png" alt="How Does Form-Based Authentication Work" class="img-fluid w-50">

        <br>
        <br>
        <ul>
          <li>Step 1: A client requests access to a protected resource</li>
          <li>Step 2: If the client is unauthenticated, the server redirects the client to a login page</li>
          <li>Step 3: The client submits the login form to the server</li>
          <li>Step 4: If the login succeeds, the server redirects the client to the resource. If the login fails, the
            client is redirected to an error page</li>
        </ul>

      </div>

      <p>To perform these tests, please navigate to this <a href="/login">page</a></p>
      <h2 id="login-automation-test-cases">Login Automation Test Cases</h2>
      <h3 id="test-case-1-successful-login">Test Case 1: Successful Login</h3>
      <ol>
        <li>Launch the browser.</li>
        <li>Navigate to the <a href="/login">login</a> page URL.</li>
        <li>Verify that the login page is displayed successfully.</li>
        <li>Enter <strong>Username</strong>: <code>practice</code>.</li>
        <li>Enter <strong>Password</strong>: <code>SuperSecretPassword!</code>.</li>
        <li>Click the <strong>Login</strong> button.</li>
        <li>Verify that the user is redirected to the <code>/secure</code> page.</li>
        <li>Confirm the success message "You logged into a secure area!" is visible.</li>
        <li>Verify that a <strong>Logout</strong> button is displayed.</li>
      </ol>
      <hr>
      <h3 id="test-case-2-invalid-username">Test Case 2: Invalid Username</h3>
      <ol>
        <li>Launch the browser.</li>
        <li>Navigate to the login page URL.</li>
        <li>Verify that the login page is displayed successfully.</li>
        <li>Enter an incorrect <strong>Username</strong> (e.g., <code>wrongUser</code>).</li>
        <li>Enter <strong>Password</strong>: <code>SuperSecretPassword!</code>.</li>
        <li>Click the <strong>Login</strong> button.</li>
        <li>Verify that an error message "Invalid username." is displayed.</li>
        <li>Ensure the user remains on the login page.</li>
      </ol>
      <hr>
      <h3 id="test-case-3-invalid-password">Test Case 3: Invalid Password</h3>
      <ol>
        <li>Launch the browser.</li>
        <li>Navigate to the login page URL.</li>
        <li>Verify that the login page is displayed successfully.</li>
        <li>Enter <strong>Username</strong>: <code>practice</code>.</li>
        <li>Enter an incorrect <strong>Password</strong> (e.g., <code>WrongPassword</code>).</li>
        <li>Click the <strong>Login</strong> button.</li>
        <li>Verify that an error message "Invalid password." is displayed.</li>
        <li>Ensure the user remains on the login page.</li>
      </ol>




    </div>
